[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Start Tag      ] <span id="Comments">
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span id="comments">
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] Comments:
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <div dir="ltr" class="mw-geshi mw-code mw-content-ltr">
[Start Tag      ] <div class="html4strict source-html4strict">
[Start Tag      ] <pre class="de1 hljs xml">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="sc-1">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-comment">
[Text           ] &lt;!-- This is a comment --&gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </pre>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] Comments can help in the understanding of the markup and do not display in the webpage.
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] There are several types of markup elements used in HTML:
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <dl>
[Start Tag      ] <dt>
[Text           ] Structural markup describes the purpose of text
[End Tag        ] </dt>
[Start Tag      ] <dd>
[Text           ] For example,
[Start Tag      ] <code class="nowrap" style>
[Text           ] &lt;h2&gt;Golf&lt;/h2&gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] establishes "Golf" as a second-level
[Start Tag      ] <a href="http://www.wikiwand.com/en/HTML_element#Basic_text" title="HTML element" class="int-link">
[Text           ] heading
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] . Structural markup does not denote any specific rendering, but most web browsers have default styles for element formatting. Content may be further styled using
[Start Tag      ] <a href="http://www.wikiwand.com/en/Cascading_Style_Sheets" title="Cascading Style Sheets" class="int-link">
[Text           ] Cascading Style Sheets
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] (CSS).
[Start Tag      ] <sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference">
[Start Tag      ] <a href="http://www.wikiwand.com/en/HTML#citenote49" class="anch-link">
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 49
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[End Tag        ] </dd>
[Start Tag      ] <dt>
[Text           ] Presentational markup describes the appearance of the text, regardless of its purpose
[End Tag        ] </dt>
[Start Tag      ] <dd>
[Text           ] For example
[Start Tag      ] <code class="nowrap" style>
[Text           ] &lt;b&gt;boldface&lt;/b&gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] indicates that visual output devices should render "boldface" in bold text, but gives little indication what devices that are unable to do this (such as aural devices that read the text aloud) should do. In the case of both
[Start Tag      ] <code class="nowrap" style>
[Text           ] &lt;b&gt;bold&lt;/b&gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] and
[Start Tag      ] <code class="nowrap" style>
[Text           ] &lt;i&gt;italic&lt;/i&gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] , there are other elements that may have equivalent visual renderings but which are more semantic in nature, such as
[Start Tag      ] <code class="nowrap" style>
[Text           ] &lt;strong&gt;strong text&lt;/strong&gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] and
[Start Tag      ] <code class="nowrap" style>
[Text           ] &lt;em&gt;emphasised text&lt;/em&gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] respectively. It is easier to see how an aural user agent should interpret the latter two elements. However, they are not equivalent to their presentational counterparts: it would be undesirable for a screen-reader to emphasize the name of a book, for instance, but on a screen such a name would be italicized. Most presentational markup elements have become
[Start Tag      ] <a href="http://www.wikiwand.com/en/Deprecation" title="Deprecation" class="int-link">
[Text           ] deprecated
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] under the HTML 4.0 specification in favor of using
[Start Tag      ] <a href="http://www.wikiwand.com/en/Cascading_Style_Sheets" title="Cascading Style Sheets" class="int-link">
[Text           ] CSS
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] for styling.
[End Tag        ] </dd>
[Start Tag      ] <dt>
[Text           ] Hypertext markup makes parts of a document into links to other documents
[End Tag        ] </dt>
[Start Tag      ] <dd>
[Text           ] An anchor element creates a
[Start Tag      ] <a href="http://www.wikiwand.com/en/Hyperlink" title="Hyperlink" class="int-link">
[Text           ] hyperlink
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] in the document and its
[Start Tag      ] <code>
[Text           ] href
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] attribute sets the link's target
[Start Tag      ] <a href="http://www.wikiwand.com/en/Uniform_Resource_Locator" title="Uniform Resource Locator" class="mw-redirect int-link">
[Text           ] URL
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] . For example the HTML markup,
[Start Tag      ] <code class="nowrap" style>
[Text           ] &lt;a href="http://www.google.com/"&gt;Wikipedia&lt;/a&gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] , will render the word "
[Start Tag      ] <span class="plainlinks">
[Start Tag      ] <a rel="nofollow" class="external text ext-link" href="http://www.google.com/" target="_blank">
[Text           ] Wikipedia
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] " as a hyperlink. To render an image as a hyperlink, an "img" element is inserted as content into the "a" element. Like "br", "img" is an empty element with attributes but no content or closing tag.
[Start Tag      ] <code class="nowrap" style>
[Text           ] &lt;a href="http://example.org"&gt;
[Start Tag      ] <code class="nowrap" style>
[Text           ] &lt;img src="image.gif" alt="descriptive text" width="50" height="50" border="0"&gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] &lt;/a&gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] .
[End Tag        ] </dd>
[End Tag        ] </dl>
[Start Tag      ] <h4>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="mw-headline" id="Attributes">
[Text           ] Attributes
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </h4>
[Start Tag      ] <table class="section_info">
[Start Tag      ] <tbody>
[Start Tag      ] <tr>
[Start Tag      ] <td class="icon">
[Start Tag      ] <i>
[End Tag        ] </i>
[End Tag        ] </td>
[Start Tag      ] <td>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] Main article:
[Start Tag      ] <a href="http://www.wikiwand.com/en/HTML_attribute" title="HTML attribute" class="int-link">
[Text           ] HTML attribute
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </p>
[End Tag        ] </td>
[End Tag        ] </tr>
[End Tag        ] </tbody>
[End Tag        ] </table>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] Most of the attributes of an element are
[Start Tag      ] <a href="http://www.wikiwand.com/en/Attribute-value_pair" title="Attribute-value pair" class="mw-redirect int-link">
[Text           ] name-value pairs
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] , separated by "=" and written within the start tag of an element after the element's name. The value may be enclosed in single or double quotes, although values consisting of certain characters can be left unquoted in HTML (but not XHTML) .
[Start Tag      ] <sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference">
[Start Tag      ] <a href="http://www.wikiwand.com/en/HTML#citenote50" class="anch-link">
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 50
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Start Tag      ] <sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference">
[Start Tag      ] <a href="http://www.wikiwand.com/en/HTML#citenote51" class="anch-link">
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 51
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] Leaving attribute values unquoted is considered unsafe.
[Start Tag      ] <sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference">
[Start Tag      ] <a href="http://www.wikiwand.com/en/HTML#citenote52" class="anch-link">
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 52
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] In contrast with name-value pair attributes, there are some attributes that affect the element simply by their presence in the start tag of the element,
[Start Tag      ] <sup id="cite_ref-tagshtml_6-2" class="reference">
[Start Tag      ] <a href="http://www.wikiwand.com/en/HTML#citenotetagshtml6" class="anch-link">
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 6
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] like the
[Start Tag      ] <code>
[Text           ] ismap
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] attribute for the
[Start Tag      ] <code>
[Text           ] img
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] element.
[Start Tag      ] <sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference">
[Start Tag      ] <a href="http://www.wikiwand.com/en/HTML#citenote53" class="anch-link">
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 53
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] There are several common attributes that may appear in many elements&nbsp;:
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <ul>
[Start Tag      ] <li>
[Text           ] The
[Start Tag      ] <code>
[Text           ] id
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] attribute provides a document-wide unique identifier for an element. This is used to identify the element so that stylesheets can alter its presentational properties, and scripts may alter, animate or delete its contents or presentation. Appended to the URL of the page, it provides a globally unique identifier for the element, typically a sub-section of the page. For example, the ID "Attributes" in
[Start Tag      ] <code>
[Text           ] http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML#Attributes
[End Tag        ] </code>
[End Tag        ] </li>
[Start Tag      ] <li>
[Text           ] The
[Start Tag      ] <code>
[Text           ] class
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] attribute provides a way of classifying similar elements. This can be used for
[Start Tag      ] <a href="http://www.wikiwand.com/en/Semantics" title="Semantics" class="int-link">
[Text           ] semantic
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] or presentation purposes. For example, an HTML document might semantically use the designation
[Start Tag      ] <code>
[Text           ] class="notation"
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] to indicate that all elements with this class value are subordinate to the main text of the document. In presentation, such elements might be gathered together and presented as footnotes on a page instead of appearing in the place where they occur in the HTML source. Class attributes are used semantically in
[Start Tag      ] <a href="http://www.wikiwand.com/en/Microformat" title="Microformat" class="int-link">
[Text           ] microformats
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] . Multiple class values may be specified; for example
[Start Tag      ] <code>
[Text           ] class="notation important"
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] puts the element into both the "notation" and the "important" classes.
[End Tag        ] </li>
[Start Tag      ] <li>
[Text           ] An author may use the
[Start Tag      ] <code>
[Text           ] style
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] attribute to assign presentational properties to a particular element. It is considered better practice to use an element's
[Start Tag      ] <code>
[Text           ] id
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] or
[Start Tag      ] <code>
[Text           ] class
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] attributes to select the element from within a stylesheet, though sometimes this can be too cumbersome for a simple, specific, or ad hoc styling.
[End Tag        ] </li>
[Start Tag      ] <li>
[Text           ] The
[Start Tag      ] <code>
[Text           ] title
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] attribute is used to attach subtextual explanation to an element. In most browsers this attribute is displayed as a
[Start Tag      ] <a href="http://www.wikiwand.com/en/Tooltip" title="Tooltip" class="int-link">
[Text           ] tooltip
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] .
[End Tag        ] </li>
[Start Tag      ] <li>
[Text           ] The
[Start Tag      ] <code>
[Text           ] lang
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] attribute identifies the natural language of the element's contents, which may be different from that of the rest of the document. For example, in an English-language document:
[Start Tag      ] <div dir="ltr" class="mw-geshi mw-code mw-content-ltr">
[Start Tag      ] <div class="html4strict source-html4strict">
[Start Tag      ] <pre class="de1 hljs xml">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="sc2">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Text           ] &lt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="kw2">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-title">
[Text           ] p
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] Oh well,
[Start Tag      ] <span class="sc2">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Text           ] &lt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="kw2">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-title">
[Text           ] span
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="kw3">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-attribute">
[Text           ] lang
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="sy0">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Text           ] =
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="st0">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-value">
[Text           ] "fr"
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] c'est la vie
[Start Tag      ] <span class="sc2">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Text           ] &lt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="sy0">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Text           ] /
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="kw2">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-title">
[Text           ] span
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] , as they say in France.
[Start Tag      ] <span class="sc2">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Text           ] &lt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="sy0">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Text           ] /
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="kw2">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-title">
[Text           ] p
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </pre>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[End Tag        ] </li>
[End Tag        ] </ul>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] The abbreviation element,
[Start Tag      ] <code>
[Text           ] abbr
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] , can be used to demonstrate some of these attributes&nbsp;:
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <div dir="ltr" class="mw-geshi mw-code mw-content-ltr">
[Start Tag      ] <div class="html4strict source-html4strict">
[Start Tag      ] <pre class="de1 hljs xml">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="sc2">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Text           ] &lt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="kw2">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-title">
[Text           ] abbr
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="kw3">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-attribute">
[Text           ] id
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="sy0">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Text           ] =
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="st0">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-value">
[Text           ] "anId"
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="kw3">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-attribute">
[Text           ] class
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="sy0">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Text           ] =
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="st0">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-value">
[Text           ] "jargon"
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="kw3">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-attribute">
[Text           ] style
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="sy0">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Text           ] =
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="st0">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-value">
[Text           ] "color:purple;"
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[End Tag        ] </span>

[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="sy0">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Text           ] =
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="st0">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-value">

[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class="hljs-tag">
